          <title>Thinking, Resting, Working, Taking some time off<title/>
          <link>http://feed.phlow-magazine.com/~r/phlow-magazine/~3/1vQGiMDYkU4/1701-thinking-resting-working-taking-some-time-off<link/>
          <comments>http://phlow-magazine.com/news/1701-thinking-resting-working-taking-some-time-off#comments<comments/>
          <pubDate>Mon, 06 Sep 2010 20:55:20 +0000<pubDate/>
          <dc:creator>acoustic_junkie@web.de (mo.)<dc:creator/>
          <category>News<category/>
          <guid isPermaLink="false" >http://phlow-magazine.com/?p=1701<guid/>
          <description>Dear reader! Currently we're under a little bit of stress. Phlow-Magazine.com is a fun project. The main editors Sven Swift and mo. got a boy and a girl recently and they care a lot of those little ones. Meanwhile Sven pushes hardly his netlabel Error Broadcast together with his mate Flip, while mo. works on [...]<description/>
          <content:encoded><p>Dear reader!</p> <p>Currently we're under a little bit of stress. Phlow-Magazine.com is a fun project. The main editors Sven Swift and mo. got a boy and a girl recently and they care a lot of those little ones. Meanwhile Sven pushes hardly his netlabel <strong><a href="http://error-broadcast.com">Error Broadcast</a></strong> together with his mate Flip, while mo. works on a relaunch of <strong><a href="http://www.netlabels.org">Netlabels.org</a></strong>. Currently these projects have the highest priority.</p> <p>At the same time we do Phlow and Netlabels.org mainly for fun. We don't earn serious money with our beloved blog and netlabel catalogue. But unfortunately we need money to life, to feed our children.</p> <p>Please be patient... we will return soon, we still love and listen to lots of music but have not the time to write about. But there are three possibilities: Connect with us via <strong><a href="http://twitter.com/phlow" target="_blank">Twitter</a></strong>, subscribe to our newsletter or grab <strong><a href="http://feed.phlow-magazine.com/phlow-magazine">our RSS-Feed</a></strong>. If there will be new content, you get posted!</p> <p>Till then, just dig into <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/free-mp3-music-download"><strong>our archive</strong></a> with more than 200 reviews or visit our spanish brothers from <a href="http://Phlow.es"><strong>Phlow.es</strong></a>.</p> <p>Greets and Beats from Cologne, the Phlow Team</p> No tags for this post. <h4>Related posts</h4> <ul           <title>Join us @ Cologne Commons 2010<title/>
          <link>http://feed.phlow-magazine.com/~r/phlow-magazine/~3/k_5rWLDoTM0/1698-join-us-cologne-commons-2010<link/>
          <comments>http://phlow-magazine.com/feature/1698-join-us-cologne-commons-2010#comments<comments/>
          <pubDate>Wed, 02 Jun 2010 07:49:52 +0000<pubDate/>
          <dc:creator>acoustic_junkie@web.de (mo.)<dc:creator/>

          <description><strong>Conference &#38; Festival for Digital Culture</strong> &#124; For the second time we teamed up with friends in Cologne to organise another Cologne Commons. This year our slogan is <em>be shareful!</em> and we opened the focus on digital culture in general. We invite you to come to our wonderful city from 10th to 12th of June 2010. We offer you three days of knowledge and culture. The curtain falls with the <a href="http://cologne-commons.de/kinoabend" target="_blank">cinema evening</a> at thursday showing you some of the finest creative commons movies around. On friday and saturday we open your mind and share ideas, knowledge and discuss the future of copyrights, the print media or the state of privacy during our <a href="http://cologne-commons.de/konferenz/546-jurgen-ertelt" target="_blank">conference</a>. While all speeches and discussions will be in english, we have one special panel for you with your favorite netaudio heroes. We called it "Hello world, my name is Netaudio!". In the evening we invited once again musicians from all over Europe, even from Chile, South America to rock the <a href="http://cologne-commons.de/festival" target="_blank">music festival</a>. So pick up a <a href="http://cologne-commons.de/ticket">ticket</a> at our digital counter and don't miss our two free compilations featuring wonderful music and the artists of the festival. So check out our <a href="http://cologne-commons.de/musik-video-downloads/664-cologne-commons-compilation-05" target="_blank">free compilations</a> Cologne Commons 05 and Cologne Commons 04! <strong>And please become a fan on <a href="http://www.facebook.com/colognecommons">www.facebook.com/colognecommons</a>!</strong><description/>

On friday and saturday we open your mind and share ideas, knowledge and discuss the future of copyrights, the print media or the state of privacy during our <a href="http://cologne-commons.de/konferenz/546-jurgen-ertelt" target="_blank">conference</a>.           <title>map~map â€“ â€œFor Friends This Winterâ€<title/>
          <link>http://feed.phlow-magazine.com/~r/phlow-magazine/~3/qEobEs1dk2k/1692-mapmap-for-friends-this-winter<link/>
          <comments>http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/ambient/1692-mapmap-for-friends-this-winter#comments<comments/>
          <pubDate>Wed, 12 May 2010 19:04:33 +0000<pubDate/>
          <dc:creator>acoustic_junkie@web.de (mo.)<dc:creator/>
          <category>Ambient<category/>

          <description>Minimal Ambient &#124; A tiny EP is stolen from a blog called "Dust Breeding" which I love a lot. These terribly short however mesmerizing sketches of minimal Ambient and musical processing of environmental noise are something I come back to on a regular basis. As the title already suggests, "For Friends This Winter" is quite [...]<description/>
          <content:encoded><p><strong><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/mapmap_ep_cover.jpg"><img src="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/mapmap_ep_cover-250x250.jpg" class="alignleft size-medium wp-image-1693" alt="" width="250" height="250" /></a>Minimal Ambient</strong> | A tiny EP is stolen from a blog called "Dust Breeding" which I love a lot. These terribly short however mesmerizing sketches of minimal Ambient and musical processing of environmental noise are something I come back to on a regular basis. As the title already suggests, "For Friends This Winter" is quite an intimate thing, and evertime I listen to it it feels a bit like stalking someone.<br /> <!--mp3links--><br /> <a href="http://rubored.org/phlow_magazine/map-map_-_090611.mp3">map~map - "09-06-11"</a> (MP3)<br /> <a href="http://rubored.org/phlow_magazine/map-map_-_091117.mp3">map~map- "09-11-17"</a> (MP3)<br /> <a href="http://rubored.org/phlow_magazine/map-map_-_090919.mp3">map~map- "09-09-19"</a> (MP3)<br /> <!--mp3linksend--></p> <p><span id="more-1692"></span></p> <p><br /><script type="text/javascript"><!-- google_ad_client = "pub-9843281692245770"; /* Phlow_Mag_Vor_Artikel_336x280 */ google_ad_slot = "0860514354"; google_ad_width = 336; google_ad_height = 280; //--> </script> <script type="text/javascript" src="http://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/show_ads.js"> </script><br /><br /></p> <p>"Dust Breeding" is the daily blog Marc Fisher is running in his second year now. Fisher lives in beautyful Portland, is 50% of <a href="http://unrecnow.com/">Unrecognizable Now</a> and 100% of map~map. Very much what "blogs" used to be in the heyday of the interweb, "Dust Breeding" is aboutÂ  posting something every day, typically photos and a few personal words. You can find spontaneous recordings, sound experiments and jam sessions there posted, too. This is entertaining at least, inspiring and memorable at best.</p> <p><a href="http://unrecnow.com/dust/2182">"For Friends This Winter"</a> was posted the 23. of December 2009. <strong>Six little compositions that engage you with subtle drones and cyclic motives of something that once was melody.</strong> The mood is dark chesnut with a hint of cosy russet. A wonderful and peaceful collection that goes perfectly well with <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/ambient/1673-geotic-hearth">Geotic</a> or <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/ambient/1669-maps-and-diagrams-the-giant-woods-yuki-yaki">Maps and Diagrams</a>, to name just my most recent posts in the Ambient-genre.           <itunes:subtitle>Minimal Ambient | A tiny EP is stolen from a blog called "Dust Breeding" which I love a lot. These terribly short however mesmerizing sketches of minimal Ambient and musical processing of environmental noise are something I come back to on a regular ba...<itunes:subtitle/>
          <itunes:summary>(http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/mapmap_ep_cover-250x250.jpg)Minimal Ambient | A tiny EP is stolen from a blog called "Dust Breeding" which I love a lot. These terribly short however mesmerizing sketches of minimal Ambient and musical processing of environmental noise are something I come back to on a regular basis. As the title already suggests, "For Friends This Winter" is quite an intimate thing, and evertime I listen to it it feels a bit like stalking someone. map~map - "09-06-11" (http://rubored.org/phlow_magazine/map-map_-_090611.mp3) (MP3) map~map- "09-11-17" (http://rubored.org/phlow_magazine/map-map_-_091117.mp3) (MP3) map~map- "09-09-19" (http://rubored.org/phlow_magazine/map-map_-_090919.mp3) (MP3) "Dust Breeding" is the daily blog Marc Fisher is running in his second year now. Fisher lives in beautyful Portland, is 50% of Unrecognizable Now (http://unrecnow.com/) and 100% of map~map. Very much what "blogs" used to be in the heyday of the interweb, "Dust Breeding" is aboutÂ  posting something every day, typically photos and a few personal words. You can find spontaneous recordings, sound experiments and jam sessions there posted, too. This is entertaining at least, inspiring and memorable at best. "For Friends This Winter" (http://unrecnow.com/dust/2182) was posted the 23. of December 2009. Six little compositions that engage you with subtle drones and cyclic motives of something that once was melody. The mood is dark chesnut with a hint of cosy russet. A wonderful and peaceful collection that goes perfectly well with Geotic (http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/ambient/1673-geotic-hearth) or Maps and Diagrams (http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/ambient/1669-maps-and-diagrams-the-giant-woods-yuki-yaki), to name just my most recent posts in the Ambient-genre. Love.           <content:encoded><p><strong><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/pm015.jpg"><img src="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/pm015-250x250.jpg" class="align left size-medium wp-image-1690" alt="" width="250" height="250" /></a>How to make a foreign song your own</strong> | Friends, Bettina Rhymes is back to the review biz! Let us celebrate this return to form with a WONDERFUL little gem of a Pop record: Montag aka Antoine BÃ©dard is a well-decorated Canadian songwriter who delivers five coverversions of 80s/ 90s Indiepop that will crack your stony hearts. Alas!</p> <p><!--mp3links--><br /> <a href="http://storage.peppermillrecords.com/montag/01-No_Aloha_(The_Breeders_cover).mp3">Montag - "No Aloah" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://storage.peppermillrecords.com/montag/02-Set_Adrift_a_Memory_of_You_(PM_Dawn_cover).mp3">Montag - "Set Adrift a Memory of You" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://storage.peppermillrecords.com/montag/03-Angel_I_Will_Walk_You_Home_(Unrest_cover).mp3">Montag - "Angel I will Walk You Home" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://storage.peppermillrecords.com/montag/04-Small_Town_Boy-Never_Gonna_Cry_Again_(Bronksi_Beat-Eurythmics_cover).mp3">Montag - "Small Town Boy / Never Gonna Cry Again" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://storage.peppermillrecords.com/montag/05-Sunflower_(Low_cover).mp3">Montag - "Sunflower" (MP3)</a><br /> <!--mp3linksend--></p> <p><span id="more-1689"></span></p> <p><br /><script type="text/javascript"><!-- google_ad_client = "pub-9843281692245770"; /* Phlow_Mag_Vor_Artikel_336x280 */ google_ad_slot = "0860514354"; google_ad_width = 336; google_ad_height = 280; //--> </script> <script type="text/javascript" src="http://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/show_ads.js"> </script><br /><br /></p> <p>It is good practice at <a href="http://www.peppermillrecords.com/">Peppermill Records</a> not to make to many words about their releases. Typically this is not necessary as every releases speaks for itself, and this is especially true when you consider Montags' <a href="http://www.peppermillrecords.com/pm015">"Des Cassettes et un Walkman Jaune"</a>.</p> <p>Montag is Vancouver-based <a href="http://www.montag.ca/" target="_blank">Antoine BÃ©dard</a>. <strong>On this little EP, the man reworks adolescence favourites in his very own styles of warm synth arrangements, leftfield singing and Disco beats.</strong> We get to hear popular songs by <em>PM Dawn</em>, <em>Bronski Beat</em> and <em>Eurythmics </em>as well as a <em>Breeders</em>, <em>Unrest</em> and <em>Low</em> cover.</p> <p>Interestingly, the 90s songs and the 80s songs go together very well. This is mainly because Antoine makes the tender Indierock of the likes named atop sound 80s whilst leaving his Synthpop idols rather untouched. One might criticize this as too soft and artless. Myself I enjoy the lush and nostalgic melodies and meanwhile consider the possibility to purchase his latest album <a href="http://www.allmusic.com/cg/amg.dll?p=amg&amp;sql=10:dvfuxzy5ldde~T00">"Going Places"</a>.</p> <h2>MP3 POP Music Download</h2> <p><strong>Download:</strong> <a href="http://storage.peppermillrecords.com/montag/Montag-Des_cassettes_et_un_Walkman_jaune.zip">"Des Cassettes et un           <description>Tribute to Pop &#124; The album Numbskull by Lord Lumb is an unashamed celebration by an artist of his heroes.Â With name checks going to David Bowie, Iggy Pop, Lou Reed, Debbie Harry, his Lordship lays his cards of inspiration on the table within the first few lines of the opening track â&#8364;&#339;I Dream Of Bowieâ&#8364;&#157;. [...]<description/>
          <content:encoded><p><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/cover_numbskull.jpg"><img src="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/cover_numbskull-250x250.jpg" alt="" title="cover_numbskull" width="250" height="250" class="alignleft size-medium wp-image-1677" /></a><strong>Tribute to Pop</strong> | The album Numbskull by Lord Lumb is an unashamed celebration by an artist of his heroes.Â With name checks going to David Bowie, Iggy Pop, Lou Reed, Debbie Harry, his Lordship lays his cards of inspiration on the table within the first few lines of the opening track â&#8364;&#339;I Dream Of Bowieâ&#8364;&#157;. This excellent piece of bouncing electronic pop rock, the result I am told of a dream about David Bowie, sets the scene for an album that is crammed with refreshing songs whose origins in the electronic music of the late 1970s is clear.Â </p> <p><!--mp3links--><br /> <a href="http://www.svcrecords.co.uk/promo/lord_numb__eileen.mp3">Lord Numb - "Eileen" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.svcrecords.co.uk/promo/lord_numb__bowie.mp3">Lord Numb - "I Dream of Bowie" (MP3)</a><br /> <!--mp3linksend--></p> <p><span id="more-1678"></span></p> <p><!--adsense--></p> <p>And Lord Numb certainly knows how to write songs. "A Man With A ? For A Face" skips along with Lord Numbâ&#8364;&#8482;s trade mark combination of edgy live guitar and monophonic analogue synth sounds, driven by an urgent and mechanized drum beat.</p> <p>However, this is certainly no exercise in Heritage Electronica. The gritty "Cubitt", with its classic synth sounds and flat distorted guitars, is a good example of a track where Lord Numb makes good use of momentary glitches and contemporary production values to ensure that this is definitely an album for the Twenty First Century.</p> <p>The floating and resonant "Never Going Home" brings down the tempo, mining similar territory to David Bowieâ&#8364;&#8482;s Space Oddity, with itâ&#8364;&#8482;s references to being lost in space far away from home.</p> <p>This is an album both dark and humorous, that contains surprising juxtapositions of the familiar and the strange. The natural, often represented by the human voice and the guitar, is deployed as a taught counterpoint to electronic and machine sounds. Lord Numbâ&#8364;&#8482;s undoubted talent as a songsmith provides an able frame work upon which lie layers and layers of intoxicating sound.</p> <p>Like his hero, David Bowie, who at the height of his powers could mould an unfamiliar shape into catchy tune and, conversely, mutate a catchy tune into an unfamiliar shape, Numb is a master of the hook and the contorted sound. In this album he builds on his earlier material, like "Pipistrelle", to produce a sound that, while referencing his heroes such as Bowie, Devo, Magazine and Neu (to name but a few), is distinctly Lord Numb.</p> <p>What I love most about this album is its clarity of purpose, its concise approach to music making. There are no drifting, meandering, self indulgent tracks lasting 10 minutes or more, so often the curse of modern electronic music. There is no waste or waffle. The longest track tops out at a neat four minutes and seven seconds. This is a gem of an album.</p> <h2>MP3 Pop Music Download</h2> <p><strong>Download:</strong> <a href="http://www.svcrecords.co.uk/releases/lord_numb__numbskull.zip">Lord Numb - "Numbskull" (ZIP-Archive)</a><br /> <strong>Artist-Website:</strong> <a href="http://www.myspace.com/lordynumb">www.myspace.com/lordynumb</a><br /> <strong>Release:</strong> <a href="http://www.svcrecords.co.uk/artist_lord_numb.html">Lord Numb - "Numbskull"</a><br /> <strong>Netlabel:</strong> <a href="http://www.svcrecords.co.uk">www.svcrecords.co.uk</a></p> Tags: <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/lord-numb" title="Lord Numb" rel="tag">Lord Numb</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/svc-records" title="svc records" rel="tag">svc records</a><br /> <h4>Related posts</h4> <ul class="st-related-posts"> <li>No related posts.</li> </ul> <p><a href="http://feedads.g.doubleclick.net/~a/zsSq_cj8UxKpiIfC7VCv44IZR-I/0/da"><img src="http://feedads.g.doubleclick.net/~a/zsSq_cj8UxKpiIfC7VCv44IZR-I/0/di" border="0" ismap="true"></img></a><br/> <a href="http://feedads.g.doubleclick.net/~a/zsSq_cj8UxKpiIfC7VCv44IZR-I/1/da"><img src="http://feedads.g.doubleclick.net/~a/zsSq_cj8UxKpiIfC7VCv44IZR-I/1/di" border="0" ismap="true"></img></a></p><div class="feedflare"> <a href="http://feed.phlow-magazine.com/~ff/phlow-magazine?a=9LIA_u3kuA4:y0dDF_6-r3A:yIl2AUoC8zA"><img src="http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/phlow-magazine?d=yIl2AUoC8zA" border="0"></img></a> <a href="http://feed.phlow-magazine.com/~ff/phlow-magazine?a=9LIA_u3kuA4:y0dDF_6-r3A:V_sGLiPBpWU"><img src="http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/phlow-magazine?i=9LIA_u3kuA4:y0dDF_6-r3A:V_sGLiPBpWU" border="0"></img></a> <a href="http://feed.phlow-magazine.com/~ff/phlow-magazine?a=9LIA_u3kuA4:y0dDF_6-r3A:F7zBnMyn0Lo"><img src="http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/phlow-magazine?i=9LIA_u3kuA4:y0dDF_6-r3A:F7zBnMyn0Lo" border="0"></img></a> <a href="http://feed.phlow-magazine.com/~ff/phlow-magazine?a=9LIA_u3kuA4:y0dDF_6-r3A:dnMXMwOfBR0"><img src="http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/phlow-magazine?d=dnMXMwOfBR0" border="0"></img></a> <a href="http://feed.phlow-magazine.com/~ff/phlow-magazine?a=9LIA_u3kuA4:y0dDF_6-r3A:gIN9vFwOqvQ"><img src="http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/phlow-magazine?i=9LIA_u3kuA4:y0dDF_6-r3A:gIN9vFwOqvQ" border="0"></img></a> </div><img src="http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/phlow-magazine/~4/9LIA_u3kuA4" height="1" width="1"/><content:encoded/>

          <content:encoded><p><strong><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/Hearth.jpg"><img src="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/Hearth-250x250.jpg" alt="" class="size-medium wp-image-1674 alignleft" width="250" height="250" /></a>Warm Drones</strong> | <strong>Geotic</strong> is the Ambient music outfit of Anticon recording artist <strong>Baths</strong> who is active as <strong>Postfoetus</strong>, too. While Baths is biased towards Brainfeeder-style Hip Hop and Postfoetus can clearly be attributed to beatladen Electronica, <strong>Geotic</strong> is all about blurry, harmonious Ambient music. California dreaming...</p> <p><!--mp3links--><br /> <a href="http://rubored.org/phlow_magazine/geotic_03.mp3"> Geotic - "Smiles and Experiments In The Vanilla Kitchen"</a><br /> <a href="http://rubored.org/phlow_magazine/geotic_09.mp3">Geotic - "Sleeping Forever; We're Gods On Miles Of Clouds"</a><br /> <a href="http://rubored.org/phlow_magazine/geotic_10.mp3">Geotic - "I'm Learning Who You Are"</a><br /> <!--mp3linksend--></p> <p><span id="more-1673"></span></p> <p><!--adsense--></p> <p>Behind all these monikers is Californian native Will Wiesenfeld (what a name!). His latest <strong><a href="http://www.angelfire.com/indie/postfoetus/geotic.html">Geotic</a></strong> album "Hearth" was recorded in-between Christmas and New Years Eve 2009. Maybe this is why these ten tracks feel so calm and peaceful, light-minded and warm.</p> <p>Composed with not essentially more than a guitar, a few keys and vocals, Wiesenfeld manages to deliver an album that is rich in sound and texture but also offers <em>musical</em> qualities many musicians could learn from. "Hearth" may sound like <a href="http://allmusic.com/cg/amg.dll?p=amg&amp;sql=11:hifixqe5ldte">My Bloody Valentine</a> or <a href="http://allmusic.com/cg/amg.dll?p=amg&amp;sql=11:kvfqxq8gld6e">Stars of the Lid</a> every now and then but remains perfectly unique below the line. Real big, I mean it.</p> <p>Beautiful art comes from <a href="http://www.judewiesenfeld.com/">June Wiesenfeld</a>.</p> <h2>MP3 Ambient Music Download</h2> <p><strong>Download: <a href="http://www.mediafire.com/?yimmy1gmd5r">mediafire.com/?yimmy1gmd5r</a></strong><br /> <strong>Artist-Website: <a href="http://www.myspace.com/geoticmusic">myspace.com/geoticmusic</a></strong></p> Tags: <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/ambient" title="Ambient" rel="tag">Ambient</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/baths" title="Baths" rel="tag">Baths</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/download" title="download" rel="tag">download</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/free" title="free" rel="tag">free</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/geotic" title="Geotic" rel="tag">Geotic</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/mp3" title="mp3" rel="tag">mp3</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/music" title="music" rel="tag">music</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/netlabel" title="netlabel" rel="tag">netlabel</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/postfoetus" title="Postfoetus" rel="tag">Postfoetus</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/will-wiesenfeld" title="Will Wiesenfeld" rel="tag">Will Wiesenfeld</a><br /> <h4>Related posts</h4> <ul class="st-related-posts"> <li><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/ambient/1072-wo0-with-the-flowered-minds-phantom-channel" title="Wo0 &#8211;           <description>Dub-Reggae Pop &#124; To be honest... I do not know much about the "A Quite Bump" Netlabel from Italy, but this could change. By coincidence this mini-album "Timeless" entered my ears and successfully took the brain - with dub and pop! Sardinia Bass Legalize - "What Can I Do For Africa" (MP3) Sardinia Bass Legalize [...]<description/>
          <content:encoded><p><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/Aqbmp024-Front-600pxl.jpg"><img src="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/Aqbmp024-Front-600pxl-250x250.jpg" alt="" width="250" height="250" class="alignleft size-medium wp-image-1672" /></a><strong>Dub-Reggae Pop</strong> | To be honest... I do not know much about the "A Quite Bump" Netlabel from Italy, but this could change. By coincidence this mini-album "Timeless" entered my ears and successfully took the brain - with dub and pop! </p> <p><!--mp3links--><br /> <a href="http://mp3.phlow.de/phlow_2010/02._sardinia_bass_legalize_-_timeless_-_what_can_i_do_for_africa_feat._vibesbrain.mp3">Sardinia Bass Legalize - "What Can I Do For Africa" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://mp3.phlow.de/phlow_2010/05._sardinia_bass_legalize_-_timeless_-_timeless_version.mp3">Sardinia Bass Legalize - "Timeless Version" (MP3)</a><br /> <!--mp3linksend--></p> <p><span id="more-1671"></span></p> <p><!--adsense--></p> <p>Although I am not that much into reggae, I like dub a lot. And this release here got a certain quality, especially with the vocals. The charismatic MC sings about Africa, peace, god, faith and love. The sound of the music is clean and charming, a little bit rusty, warm and also a bit of French niceness shines through here and there. All that makes a classical dub-record. Play it in lounges and you will make friends. I promise!</p> <p>This release contains also a remix, much more blurred and stateless than the dub orientated tracks. What I would love to have is a pure instrumental version of the track <em>"What can I do for Africa"</em>. It plays in the same league like "The Modernist", "Rockers Hi-Fi" and deep soundsystem stuff. Who knows, next time the Sardinia Bass Legalize will try something like "DJ Krush" meets "Donna Regina". I do not know much about the "A Quite Bump" Netlabel from Italy, but this could change. By coincidence this mini-album "Timeless" entered my ears and successfully took the brain - with dub and pop! Sardinia Bass Legalize - "What Can I Do For Africa" (MP3) (http://mp3.phlow.de/phlow_2010/02._sardinia_bass_legalize_-_timeless_-_what_can_i_do_for_africa_feat._vibesbrain.mp3) Sardinia Bass Legalize - "Timeless Version" (MP3) (http://mp3.phlow.de/phlow_2010/05._sardinia_bass_legalize_-_timeless_-_timeless_version.mp3) Although I am not that much into reggae, I like dub a lot. And this release here got a certain quality, especially with the vocals. The charismatic MC sings about Africa, peace, god, faith and love. The sound of the music is clean and charming, a little bit rusty, warm and also a bit of French niceness shines through here and there. All that makes a classical dub-record. Play it in lounges and you will make friends. I promise! This release contains also a remix, much more blurred and stateless than the dub orientated tracks. What I would love to have is a pure instrumental version of the track "What can I do for Africa". It plays in the same league like "The Modernist", "Rockers Hi-Fi" and deep soundsystem stuff.           <content:encoded><p><strong><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/ykyk019_cover_front.jpg"><img src="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/ykyk019_cover_front-250x250.jpg" alt="" class="size-medium wp-image-1670 alignleft" width="250" height="250" /></a>Soothing Chill</strong> | Back on track with a classic Ambient album. "Classic" like GAS, Fennesz, Eno... You know the drill.Â  Behind the Maps and Diagrams moniker is UK-based Tim Martin, who has a quite <a href="http://www.discogs.com/artist/Maps+&amp;+Diagrams">impressive back catalogue</a> with various CD, CDr, MP3 and vinyl releases. For "The Giant Woods" Martin teams up with the Yuki Yaki crew. Win-win!</p> <p><!--mp3links--><br /> <a href="http://www.yukiyaki.org/download/588/YkYk019/maps_and_diagrams/ykyk019-04_maps_and_diagrams_-_last_train_home.mp3">Maps and Diagrams - "Last Train Home" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.yukiyaki.org/download/590/YkYk019/maps_and_diagrams/ykyk019-05_maps_and_diagrams_-_navel.mp3">Maps and Diagrams - "Navel" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.yukiyaki.org/download/592/YkYk019/maps_and_diagrams/ykyk019-06_maps_and_diagrams_-_savannakhet.mp3">Maps and Diagrams - "Savannakhet" (MP3)</a></p> <p><!--mp3linksend--></p> <p><span id="more-1669"></span></p> <p><!--adsense--></p> <p>Usually it is hard to put the finger on why an Ambient album is "good". For me, richness, atmosphere and innovative sound design is important. While "<a href="http://www.yukiyaki.org/releases/YkYk019/maps-and-diagrams/The-Giant-Woods">The Giant Woods</a>" could have been transmitted in the early 70's (<em>soundwise</em>), the dense and slightly haunting <em>feel</em> of the record got me eventually. The artwork caught that impression very well - a walk through the forest at night, getting lost in a foreign town as the sun is about to settle... The chill comes on soft feet!</p> <p>Besides, the intense layering and enwinding of different textures creates a sound that allows for aural discoveries on every new listen. Something you can find with <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/ambient/555-man-of-taste-ian-d-hawgood-koen-park">Ian Hawgood</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/ambient/1406-slow-dual-box-resting-bell">Slow</a> or <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/ambient/1374-astrowind-fresh-wind-in-the-valley-of-dreams-silent-flow">Astrowind</a> as well. Dig yourselves into these nine tracks and escape for 48 gracious minutes.</p> <h2>MP3 Ambient Music Download</h2> <p><strong>Download:</strong> <a href="http://www.yukiyaki.org/download/608/YkYk019/maps_and_diagrams/ykyk019_maps_and_diagrams_-_the-giant-woods__mp3.zip">The Giant Woods (ZIP)</a><br /> <strong>Artist-Website:</strong> <a href="http://www.discogs.com/artist/Maps+&amp;+Diagrams">Maps and Diagrams</a> (@Discogs)<br /> <strong>Release:</strong> <a href="http://www.yukiyaki.org/releases/YkYk019/maps-and-diagrams/The-Giant-Woods">The Giant Woods</a><br /> <strong>Netlabel: </strong><a href="http://www.yukiyaki.org/">yukiyaki.org</a><strong> </strong></p> Tags: <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/ambient" title="Ambient" rel="tag">Ambient</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/cactus-island" title="Cactus Island" rel="tag">Cactus Island</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/download" title="download" rel="tag">download</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/free" title="free" rel="tag">free</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/handstitched" title="Handstitched" rel="tag">Handstitched</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/maps-and-diagrams" title="Maps and Diagrams" rel="tag">Maps and Diagrams</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/mp3" title="mp3" rel="tag">mp3</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/music" title="music" rel="tag">music</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/netlabel" title="netlabel" rel="tag">netlabel</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/tim-martin" title="Tim Martin" rel="tag">Tim Martin</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/yuki-yaki" title="Yuki Yaki" rel="tag">Yuki Yaki</a><br /> <h4>Related posts</h4> <ul class="st-related-posts"> <li><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/ambient/1072-wo0-with-the-flowered-minds-phantom-channel" title="Wo0 &#8211;           <content:encoded><p><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/cover_eftb_roadkill_front.jpg"><img class="alignleft size-medium wp-image-1664" title="cover_eftb_roadkill_front" src="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/cover_eftb_roadkill_front-250x250.jpg" alt="" width="250" height="250" /></a><strong>A Banjo Tribute</strong> | A tiny, coincidental discovery can open completely new horizons, save your day and drive you into a direction you've never thought about. An incident like that happened to one of our creative commons music stars: Entertainment For The Braindead. She discovered the banjo. A unique instrument associated with music styles like Dixieland Jazz or Blues. But does the banjo also sounds in the hands of an artist dedicated to soft, fragile folk songs? Yes it does! Just listen!</p> <p><!--mp3links--><br /> <a href="http://www.archive.org/download/EntertainmentForTheBraindead-Roadkillaaahh.009/03_Dry_Wood.mp3">Entertainment For The Braindead- "Dry Wood" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.archive.org/download/EntertainmentForTheBraindead-Roadkillaaahh.009/08_Pirates.mp3">Entertainment For The Braindead - "Pirates" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.archive.org/download/EntertainmentForTheBraindead-Roadkillaaahh.009/02_Roadkill.mp3">Entertainment For The Braindead - "Roadkill" (MP3)</a><br /> <!--mp3linksend--></p> <p><span id="more-1665"></span></p> <p><!--adsense--></p> <p>Julia Kotowski aka Entertainment For The Braindead got bonded by the strings of her banjo.           <description>Italian HipHop Instrumentals &#124; Homework Records represent Italys finest music if we speak about modern Hip Hop instrumentals. Like Apes on Tapes also Grillo is on the spearhead of modern beats. After his great debut called "Fireworks" the label refined his tracks with five excellent remixes. Grillo - "Brown Box (Fulgeance Remix)" (MP3) The sound [...]<description/>
          <content:encoded><p><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/cover_fireworks_grillo_remixes.png"><img src="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/cover_fireworks_grillo_remixes-250x250.png" alt="" title="cover_fireworks_grillo_remixes" width="250" height="250" class="alignleft size-medium wp-image-1661" /></a><strong>Italian HipHop Instrumentals</strong> | Homework Records represent Italys finest music if we speak about modern <a href="http://www.99centbeatz.com"><a href="http://www.99centbeatz.com">Hip Hop instrumentals</a></a>. Like <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/?s=Apes+on+Tapes">Apes on Tapes</a> also Grillo is on the spearhead of modern beats. After his great debut called "Fireworks" the label refined his tracks with five excellent remixes.</p> <p><!--mp3links--><br /> <a href="http://mp3.phlow.de/phlow_2010/02._fulgeance_-_fireworks_remixes_-_brown_box_fulgeance_interstella_funk_remix_.mp3">Grillo - "Brown Box (Fulgeance Remix)" (MP3)</a><br /> <!--mp3linksend--></p> <p><span id="more-1660"></span></p> <p><!--adsense--></p> <p>The sound of Grillo is pure, very digital and funky. On "Fireworks" we listen to crispy beats, clicks, snares and solid kicks. Most of the tracks are build on some melodic grooves. This made me rewind the album to listen again to slow movers like "Clicks" or the fantastic hit "Be aware".</p> <p>Now we get the remixes and what can I say? I like the reworks even a little bit more. Each producer kept the digital sound of Grillo but managed to throw some of his delicate herbs and skills into the bowl. Just listen to the remix of "Be Aware" of Costa. Filled with some humour we nod to a straight-into-your-face pop hook. My favorite right now is the jazzy and funky retouch of Fulgeance on "Brown Box". If this one won't make you smile and move, I don't know...</p> <p><strong>Thumbs up, once again for the skills, beats and taste of Homework Records! Italys finest!</strong></p> <h2>MP3 HipHop Music Download</h2> <p><strong>Download:</strong> <a href="http://www.homeworkrecords.net/_dl_hwr/hwr016.zip">Grillo - "Fireworks Remixes" (ZIP-Archive)</a><br /> <strong>Netlabel:</strong> <a href="http://www.homeworkrecords.net/">Homework Records</a></p> Tags: <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/apes-on-tapes" title="Apes on Tapes" rel="tag">Apes on Tapes</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/grillo" title="grillo" rel="tag">grillo</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/hip-hop-instrumentals" title="hip hop instrumentals" rel="tag">hip hop instrumentals</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/homework-records" title="homework records" rel="tag">homework records</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/instrumental" title="Instrumental" rel="tag">Instrumental</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/instrumental-hiphop" title="instrumental hiphop" rel="tag">instrumental hiphop</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/modern-beats" title="modern beats" rel="tag">modern beats</a><br /> <h4>Related posts</h4> <ul class="st-related-posts"> <li><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/hiphop/1100-instrumental-hip-hop-errorbroadcast-netlabel" title="Various &#8211;           <comments>http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/house/1655-a-new-chapter-of-acid-house#comments<comments/>
          <pubDate>Wed, 03 Mar 2010 18:12:32 +0000<pubDate/>

          <description>Aciiiiid! &#124; If we believe the peepz at Tribe Toolz today is the (un)official birthday of the fabulous Roland TB-303 synthesizer. No synthesizer - except the drummachines 808 and 909 - left such an imprint on electronic music like this monophone bassline synthie. Originally invented for musicians in need of a bassline player, the TB-303 [...]<description/>
          <content:encoded><p><img src="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/cover_toolz303-II-250x250.jpg" alt="" title="cover_toolz303-II" width="250" height="250" class="alignleft size-medium wp-image-1656" /><strong>Aciiiiid!</strong> | If we believe the peepz at Tribe Toolz today is the (un)official birthday of the fabulous Roland TB-303 synthesizer. No synthesizer - except the drummachines 808 and 909 - left such an imprint on electronic music like this monophone bassline synthie. Originally invented for musicians in need of a bassline player, the TB-303 was a real flop... Until some kids like <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Phuture">Phuture</a> get hooked by the quirky sounds of the 303. And still the kids like to torture those knobs till some phunky acid bubbles its way through the speakers.</p> <p><!--mp3links--><br /> <a href="http://www.archive.org/download/Toolz303-II_2010/Toolz303-II-05-MattiasFridell-DieKameraLaeuft.mp3">Mattias Fridell - "Die Kamera LÃ¤uft" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.archive.org/download/Toolz303-II_2010/Toolz303-II-09-DavidRamaszeder-Pattern1.mp3">David Ramaszeder - "Pattern1" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.archive.org/download/Toolz303-II_2010/Toolz303-II-15-TobiasHoermann-Acid3-4.mp3">Tobias Hoermann - "Acid 3-4" (MP3)</a></p> <p><!--mp3linksend--></p> <p><span id="more-1655"></span></p> <p><!--adsense--></p> <p>Already in 2009 Tribe Toolz released a first Acid Compilation full of tributes to the sound of the Roland TB-303.           <description>Metapop with a wink &#124; Our friend Gillicuddy returns with a new EP which is great fun t2b. Five songs that oscillate between lo-fi Folk, textural experiments in sound, and Noiserock (!). What has been planted in all his music finds its way through the soil on "The Yaouhl! Mashups" eventually: Gillicuddy is the fourth [...]<description/>
          <content:encoded><p><strong><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/ca350_02_cover_front.jpg"><img src="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/ca350_02_cover_front-250x250.jpg" class="size-medium wp-image-1653 alignleft" alt="" width="250" height="250" /></a>Metapop with a wink</strong> | Our <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/folk-acoustic/1216-gillicuddy-repeating-thoughts-zinng-zanng-resting-bell">friend</a> Gillicuddy returns with a new EP which is great fun t2b. Five songs that oscillate between lo-fi Folk, textural experiments in sound, and Noiserock (!). What has been planted in all his music finds its way through the soil on "The Yaouhl! Mashups" eventually: Gillicuddy is the fourth in line of Frank Zappa, Mike Patton, and Jim O'Rourke.</p> <p><a href="http://www.archive.org/download/ca350_g/02_de_mannetjesolifant_gaat_op_reis.mp3">Gillicuddy - "de mannetjesolifant gaat op reis naar de oostzee" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.archive.org/download/ca350_g/03_sh-dah.mp3">Gillicuddy - "sh-dah" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.archive.org/download/ca350_g/04_instrumental_2.mp3">Gillicuddy - "instrumental #2" (MP3)</a><!--mp3linksend--></p> <p><span id="more-1652"></span>What might come aleatory on first listen complies just right as soon as the concept unfolds. German songwriter <a href="http://www.gillicuddy.net/">Gillicuddy</a> combines the most different genres on a short-lived EP, typically in one song. This has been true for "<a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/pop/335-gillicuddy-shmalhans-is-kuechenmeister">Shmalhans is Kuechenmeister</a>" and "<a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/folk-acoustic/1216-gillicuddy-repeating-thoughts-zinng-zanng-resting-bell">The Repeating Thoughts</a>" but is brought to perfection only now.</p> <p>Take "de mannetjesolifant gaat op reis naar de oostzee" as an example. First part is technical Noiserock, <a href="http://allmusic.com/cg/amg.dll?p=amg&amp;sql=11:d9fexqw5ldke">Jesus Lizard</a>-style. Then <a href="http://www.gillicuddy.net/">Gillicuddy</a> slows down the Jazz and pushes the song in a direction reminiscent of <a href="http://allmusic.com/cg/amg.dll?p=amg&amp;sql=11:hifuxqr5ld0e">Sonic Youth</a>: slightly detuned guitars, decent but uneal somehow. These fade into multilayer field-recordings you are never allowed to trust. Eventually, the secret is revealed, and the elephants of the Baltic Sea make their appearance...</p> <p>This song is the wildest. However, despite the versatility, a typical atmosphere of humorous darkness comes with all songs on "<a href="http://clinicalarchives.blogspot.com/2010/01/ca350-gillicuddy-yaouhl-mashups.html">The Yaouhl! Mashups</a>". This brings forth consistency, proofs the musical craftsmanship of <a href="http://www.gillicuddy.net/">Gillicudy</a> and guarantees for great listening pleasure. His best up to now, without the slightest doubt.</p> <h2>MP3 Avantgarde Pop Music Download</h2> <p><strong>Download:</strong> <a href="http://www.archive.org/download/ca350_g/ca350_gillicuddy__the_yaouhl_mashups.zip">"The Yaouhl! Mashups"</a> (ZIP-Archive)<br /> <strong>Artist-Website:</strong> <a href="http://www.gillicuddy.net/">www.gillicuddy.net</a><br /> <strong>Release:</strong> <a href="http://clinicalarchives.blogspot.com/2010/01/ca350-gillicuddy-yaouhl-mashups.html">Gillicuddy - "The Yaouhl! Mashups"</a><br /> <strong>Netlabel:</strong> <a href="http://clinicalarchives.blogspot.com">Clinical Archives</a><strong> </strong></p> Tags: <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/avantgarde-pop" title="Avantgarde Pop" rel="tag">Avantgarde Pop</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/clinical-archives" title="Clinical Archives" rel="tag">Clinical Archives</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/download" title="download" rel="tag">download</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/experimental" title="Experimental" rel="tag">Experimental</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/folk" title="folk" rel="tag">folk</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/free" title="free" rel="tag">free</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/gillicuddy" title="Gillicuddy" rel="tag">Gillicuddy</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/mp3" title="mp3" rel="tag">mp3</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/music" title="music" rel="tag">music</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/netlabel" title="netlabel" rel="tag">netlabel</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/noiserock" title="Noiserock" rel="tag">Noiserock</a><br /> <h4>Related posts</h4> <ul class="st-related-posts"> <li><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/ambient/1072-wo0-with-the-flowered-minds-phantom-channel" title="Wo0 &#8211;           <description>Dutch HipHop, English Rap &#124; While Crookram's album "19/76" on Budabeats sounded dusty, analogue, funky and deep, the productions with his partner Sagesse shine polished and bass-loaded. With a bassdrum deep like Miami Bass and a tos of funkyness between the beats the Dutch producer makes another step in his evolution. Now I know why [...]<description/>
          <content:encoded><p><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/cover_sagesse_crookram_escape_the_ep.jpg"><img src="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/cover_sagesse_crookram_escape_the_ep-250x250.jpg" alt="" title="cover_sagesse_crookram_escape_the_ep" width="250" height="250" class="alignleft size-medium wp-image-1650" /></a><strong>Dutch HipHop, English Rap</strong> | While <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/hiphop/428-crookram-1976-budabeats">Crookram's album "19/76"</a> on Budabeats sounded dusty, analogue, funky and deep, the productions with his partner Sagesse shine polished and bass-loaded. With a bassdrum deep like Miami Bass and a tos of funkyness between the beats the Dutch producer makes another step in his evolution. Now I know why the Netherlands are such a flat land. Too much bass...</p> <p><!--mp3links--><br /> <a href="http://www.bankruptrecordings.com/bar001/01_sagesse&#038;crookram-escape.mp3">Sagesse &#038; Crookram - "Escape" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.bankruptrecordings.com/bar001/02_sagesse&#038;crookram-make_way.mp3">Sagesse &#038; Crookram - "Make Way" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.bankruptrecordings.com/bar001/03_sagesse&#038;crookram-warrior.mp3">Sagesse &#038; Crookram - "Warrior" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.bankruptrecordings.com/bar001/04_sagesse&#038;crookram-patterns_of_thought.mp3">Sagesse &#038; Crookram - "Patterns of Thought" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.bankruptrecordings.com/bar001/05_sagesse&#038;crookram-epilogue.mp3">Sagesse &#038; Crookram - "Epilogue" (MP3)</a><br /> <!--mp3linksend--></p> <p><span id="more-1649"></span></p> <p><!--adsense--></p> <p>I adore crackling samples, the collage technique of old school hiphop productions. That's why I adore so much the releases of <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/budabeats">Budabeats</a>. Crookram was the second artist who refined the catalogue. Now he starts his own netlabel Bankrupt Recordings.</p> <p>While "19/76" was epic, "The Escape EP" is pure and a great production featuring different MCs - I guess from the Netherlands. Tracks like "Patterns of Thought (ft. Wreckitnize)" were produced to walk through the city in the sunshine and get a little melancholic. What amuses me, is that I like the instrumental called "Epilogue" the best. Maybe this is the track which glues his old album on Budabeats together with his next step. Even if the whole production is skillful, I wish sometimes more edges, some little gimmicks. To me Crookram is best, when he gets melancholic and hopefully he will write for us another epilogue soon.</p> <p>PS: The onyl sad thing about this EP is... I would love to hear some real Dutch rap ;)</p> <h2>MP3 Music Download</h2> <p><strong>Download:</strong> <a href="http://www.bankruptrecordings.com/bar001/bar001.zip">Sagesse &#038; Crookram - "The Escape EP" (ZIP-Archive)</a><br /> <strong>Artist-Website:</strong> <a href="http://www.myspace.com/sagessebeats">Sagesse</a> and <a href="http://www.crookram.net/">Crookram</a><br /> <strong>Release:</strong> Sagesse &#038;           <title>Alexandre Bateiras â€“ â€œCanÃ§Ãµes da Lua Novaâ€ (Merzbau)<title/>
          <link>http://feed.phlow-magazine.com/~r/phlow-magazine/~3/TWbz-Wmk7UY/1643-alexandre-bateiras-%e2%80%93-cancoes-da-lua-nova-merzbau<link/>

          <description>This one is an oldie. In fact, almost three years passed since this was released on Merzbau. Enough time for theÂ netlabel to shut its doors - the website is still on and will be for long, so make sure you stop by and listen to the other records. What is truly remarkable on â&#8364;&#339;CanÃ§Ãµes da [...]<description/>
          <content:encoded><p><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/cover_merzbau_alexandre_bateiras.jpg"><img src="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/cover_merzbau_alexandre_bateiras-250x250.jpg" alt="" title="cover_merzbau_alexandre_bateiras" width="250" height="250" class="alignleft size-medium wp-image-1648" /></a>This one is an oldie. In fact, almost three years passed since this was released on Merzbau. Enough time for theÂ netlabel to shut its doors - the website is still on and will be for long, so make sure you stop by and listen to the other records.</p> <p>What is truly remarkable on â&#8364;&#339;CanÃ§Ãµes da Lua Novaâ&#8364;&#157; (in portuguese â&#8364;&#339;Songs of the New Moonâ&#8364;&#157;) is that these eleven songs (and an outro) were in kept in a drawer for over thirty years.</p> <p><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/01-Porto_Largo.mp3">Alexandre Bateiras - Porto Largo (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/08-Variacoes_Sobre_um_tema_Melancolico.mp3">Alexandre Bateiras - VariaÃ§Ãµes sobre um Tema MelancÃ³lico (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/11-Valsa.mp3">Alexandre Bateiras - Valsa em FÃ¡# Menor (MP3)</a></p> <p><span id="more-1643"></span></p> <p><!--adsense--></p> <p>Though Alexandre Bateiras has always been a <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_guitar" target="_blank">portuguese-guitar</a> player â&#8364;&#8220; he plays since he was 15 -, he was never concerned about releasing new songs. Well, it was only due to his son's persistence that the tracks saw daylight.</p> <p>Please make notice to the fact that you're not listening to music only, you're listening to the stories that were left behind on <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alentejo" target="_blank">Alentejo</a>'s plain (South of Portugal). Most of the songs names are real places names. And those that are not still have something important to remind us. For instance, â&#8364;&#339;Tributoâ&#8364;&#157; is as tribute to a soldier who died during the portuguese colonial war back in the 60's. Alexandre Bateiras was there, whitnessed the moment and was able to show us what happened with a few chords.</p> <p>This is instumental portuguese folk: real stories told and played with a portuguese guitar. Stories of a man and somehow of an old generation of people who lived in a quiet rural Portugal and stopped their adolescense to be part of a war.</p> <p>Regardless the history lesson, these melodies are something that anyone hardly forgets. So take your own time to listen, discover and imagine all the tiny bits of existence that this record brings to life.</p> <h2>MP3 Instrumental Music Download</h2> <p>Download: <a href="http://merzbau-label.org/ccount12/click.php?id=21">Alexandre Bateiras - "CanÃ§Ãµes da Lua Nova" (ZIP- Archive)</a><br /> Artist Website: <a href="http://www.myspace.com/bateiras">http://www.myspace.com/bateiras</a><br /> Release: <a href="http://www.merzbau-label.org/merz0027_pt.htm">Alexandre Bateiras - "CanÃ§Ãµes da Lua Nova"</a><br /> Netlabel: <a href="http://www.merzbau-label.org/">Merzbau</a></p> Tags: <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/acoustic" title="acoustic" rel="tag">acoustic</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/alexandre-bateiras" title="alexandre bateiras" rel="tag">alexandre bateiras</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/instrumental" title="Instrumental" rel="tag">Instrumental</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/merzbau" title="Merzbau" rel="tag">Merzbau</a><br /> <h4>Related posts</h4> <ul class="st-related-posts"> <li><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/ambient/611-joao-triangular-ep-merzbau" title="JoÃ£o Triangular &#8211; Enough time for theÂ netlabel to shut its doors - the website is still on and will be for long, so make sure you stop by and listen to the other records. What is truly remarkable on â€œCanÃ§Ãµes da Lua Novaâ€ (in portuguese â€œSongs of the New Moonâ€) is that these eleven songs (and an outro) were in kept in a drawer for over thirty years. Alexandre Bateiras - Porto Largo (MP3) (http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/01-Porto_Largo.mp3) Alexandre Bateiras - VariaÃ§Ãµes sobre um Tema MelancÃ³lico (MP3) (http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/08-Variacoes_Sobre_um_tema_Melancolico.mp3) Alexandre Bateiras - Valsa em FÃ¡# Menor (MP3) (http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/11-Valsa.mp3) Though Alexandre Bateiras has always been a portuguese-guitar (http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_guitar) player â€“ he plays since he was 15 -, he was never concerned about releasing new songs. Well, it was only due to his son's persistence that the tracks saw daylight. Please make notice to the fact that you're not listening to music only, you're listening to the stories that were left behind on Alentejo (http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alentejo)'s plain (South of Portugal). Most of the songs names are real places names. And those that are not still have something important to remind us. For instance, â€œTributoâ€ is as tribute to a soldier who died during the portuguese colonial war back in the 60's. Alexandre Bateiras was there, whitnessed the moment and was able to show us what happened with a few chords. This is instumental portuguese folk: real stories told and played with a portuguese guitar. Stories of a man and somehow of an old generation of people who lived in a quiet rural Portugal and stopped their adolescense to be part of a war. Regardless the history lesson, these melodies are something that anyone hardly forgets. So take your own time to listen, discover and imagine all the tiny bits of existence that this record brings to life.           <description>Electronic Folk Music &#124; News from my man Bluermutt, and it is good news! I have been a big fan of his former albums and various side projects, and the more delighted to hear that this EP will be on for free although the "Decivilize After Consumption" album was a CD release.           <content:encoded><p><strong><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/cover_bluermutt.jpg"><img src="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/cover_bluermutt-250x250.jpg" class="size-medium wp-image-1639 alignleft" alt="" width="250" height="250" /></a>Electronic Folk Music</strong> | News from my man Bluermutt, and it is good news! I have been a big fan of his former albums and various <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/hiphop/258-mickey-eats-plastic-to-kill-the-white-glamour-reworks-ep-1">side projects</a>, and the more delighted to hear that this EP will be on for free although the "<a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/news/824-prgrssbluermutt-decivilice-after-consumption-nexsound-pop">Decivilize After Consumption</a>" album was a CD release. These six tracks come off like a collection of songs rather than an EP so I reckon we get outtakes to hear - however, this does not diminish quality in any way.</p> <p><a href="http://rubored.org/phlow_magazine/Bluermutt_-_The_Broken_City.mp3">Bluermutt - "The Broken City" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://rubored.org/phlow_magazine/Bluermutt_-_Androids_Breath.mp3">Bluermutt - "Androids' Breath" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://rubored.org/phlow_magazine/Bluermutt_-_Indoor_Failure.mp3">Bluermutt - "Indoor Failure" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://rubored.org/phlow_magazine/Bluermutt_-_Single_Touch.mp3">Bluermutt - "Single Touch" (MP3)<span id="more-1638"></span></a> <!--mp3linksend--></p> <p><!--adsense--></p> <p><strong>Bluermutt</strong>'s "Dislocation (and Consequences)" EP oscillates between highly processed Folk, Krautrock and melodic Electronica. Strength to his compositions is always the strong melodies, governed by a warm and rich production. Maybe this is why I consider <strong>Bluermutt</strong> Pop music rather than anything else- albeit, Pop music with respectable edges.</p> <p>The first four tracks are breathtaking: "The Broken City" sounds like a dedusted <a href="http://allmusic.com/cg/amg.dll?p=amg&amp;sql=11:39fwxqu5ldhe">Harmonia</a> jam, ca. 1974, so full of melancholy sweetness and glittering textures. "Android's Breath" features <a href="http://allmusic.com/cg/amg.dll?p=amg&amp;sql=10:3zftxqwdld6e">Leafcutter John</a>, soul alike when it comes to "Fractal Folk". His mature yet gentle voice fits the <strong>Bluermutt</strong> sound neatlessly. Wow. "Indoor Failure" eventually is pure candy. Over a <a href="http://allmusic.com/cg/amg.dll?p=amg&amp;sql=11:dvfpxqqjldhe">Four Tet</a>-style instrumental, vocals and guitar perform a wonderful Pop melody. Ohrwurm, you were warned! On four, "Single Touch" introduces the ambient part of "The Dislocation (and Consequences)". Warm and cracking Dub, bathed in sunlit harmonies, and a lot of depth: just wonderful.</p> <p>Support <strong>Bluermutt</strong> by sending over some bucks for the download! "The Dislocation (and Consequences)" EP is available for <em>pay-as-you-like</em> via <a href="http://bluermutt.bandcamp.com/album/the-dislocation-and-consequences-ep">bandcamp</a>.</p> <h2>MP3 Electronic Pop Music Download</h2> <p><strong>Artist-Website:</strong> <a href="http://www.skyapnea.com/home_of_bluermutt/" target="_blank">skyapnea.com</a><br /> <strong>Release:</strong> <a href="http://bluermutt.bandcamp.com/album/the-dislocation-and-consequences-ep" target="_blank">Bluermutt - The Disloaction (and Consequences) EP</a><strong><br /> </strong></p> Tags: <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/bandcamp" title="bandcamp" rel="tag">bandcamp</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/bluermutt" title="Bluermutt" rel="tag">Bluermutt</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/download" title="download" rel="tag">download</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/electronica" title="electronica" rel="tag">electronica</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/folk" title="folk" rel="tag">folk</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/free" title="free" rel="tag">free</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/leafcutter-john" title="Leafcutter John" rel="tag">Leafcutter John</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/misread-records" title="Misread Records" rel="tag">Misread Records</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/mp3" title="mp3" rel="tag">mp3</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/music" title="music" rel="tag">music</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/netlabel" title="netlabel" rel="tag">netlabel</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/pop" title="Pop" rel="tag">Pop</a><br /> <h4>Related posts</h4> <ul class="st-related-posts"> <li><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/news/824-prgrssbluermutt-decivilice-after-consumption-nexsound-pop" title="Bluermutt &#8211;           <title>Stockfinster â€“ â€œDead Lineâ€ (Sutemos)<title/>
          <link>http://feed.phlow-magazine.com/~r/phlow-magazine/~3/iiDpWbZ7Xt4/1408-stockfinster-dead-line-sutemos<link/>

          <pubDate>Tue, 09 Feb 2010 11:40:21 +0000<pubDate/>
          <dc:creator>acoustic_junkie@web.de (mo.)<dc:creator/>

          <description>Epic Electronic Prog Pop &#124; The Lithuanian Netlabel Sutemos is nothing new to you most likely. We have been covering their outcome ever since. Stockfinster, all the same, is a name commonly known to fans of free music. After the debut "All Becomes Music" was released in 2005, it took four years to complete "Dead [...]<description/>
          <content:encoded><p><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/stockfinster_dead_line.jpg"><img src="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/stockfinster_dead_line-250x250.jpg" class="alignleft size-medium wp-image-1409" alt="stockfinster_dead_line" width="250" height="250" /></a><strong>Epic Electronic Prog Pop</strong> | The Lithuanian Netlabel Sutemos is nothing new to you most likely. We have been covering their outcome <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/ambient/1036-various-intelligent-toys-5-sutemos-netlabel">ever</a> <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/idm/1486-ijo-selektida-sutemos">since</a>. Stockfinster, all the same, is a name commonly known to fans of free music. After the debut "All Becomes Music" was released in 2005, it took four years to complete "Dead Line", the novel full-lenght of album of Stockfinster. A long time waiting, but worth the years without a doubt.</p> <p><a href="http://www.archive.org/download//Stockfinster.-DeadLinesutemos025/01_Push_Push.mp3">Stockfinster - "Push Push" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.archive.org/download//Stockfinster.-DeadLinesutemos025/05_Knuckle.mp3">Stockfinster - "Knuckle" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.archive.org/download//Stockfinster.-DeadLinesutemos025/06_Gold_Canyon.mp3">Stockfinster- "Gold Canyon" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.archive.org/download//Stockfinster.-DeadLinesutemos025/07_Mitglieder.mp3">Stockfinster- "Mitglieder" (MP3)</a><br /> <!--mp3linksend--><br /> <span id="more-1408"></span></p> <p><strong>Stockfinster</strong> (German for "pitch black") is the one man band of MalmÃ¶-based Sebastian Borg. In the liner notes to "Dead Line", Borg (who commonly appears as "batti") excuses himself for being unproductive and slow. However, for a 76 minutes <em>opus magnus</em>, perfectly arranged and composed like this, many musicians need a whole lifetime for. If any.</p> <p>The music of <strong>Stockfinster</strong> is a mixture of Postrock and progressive Pop, essentially enhanced by many electronic elements. There is an element of nostalgia to Borg's music that stems from his melancholic melodies and the late 90's breakbeat patterns. Several time I had to think of early <em>Lamb</em> or other forward-thinking "Trip Hop" acts. From the world of Netaudio, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/hiphop/1164-orange-crush-autumn-reflections-archaic-horizon">Orange Crush</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/electronica-indietronic/111-endlos-kein-grund-zufrieden-zu-sein-live-ep-1bit-wonder">Endless</a> or <a href="http://www.12rec.net/Release_Nic-Bommarito_Harp-Fragments_058.htm" target="_blank">Nic Bommaritio</a> might suit for comparison.</p> <p>Albeit not actually at the edge of contemporary music, <strong>Stockfinster</strong> has something more valuable to offer: timelessness. Strong, atmospheric melodies, impellent beats, and a supreme production. Should be OK for the next four years, no?</p> <p><!--adsense--></p> <h2>MP3 Pop Music Download</h2> <p><strong>Download:</strong> <a href="http://www.archive.org/download/Stockfinster.-DeadLinesutemos025/Sutemos025.zip" target="_blank">"Dead Line"</a> (ZIP-Archive)<br /> <strong>Artist-Website:</strong> <a href="http://www.stockfinster.nu/" target="_blank">stockfinster.nu</a><br /> <strong>Release:</strong> <a href="http://www.sutemos.net/en/release;gid,27" target="_blank">Stockfinster - "Dead Line"</a><br /> <strong>Netlabel: </strong><a href="http://www.sutemos.net/" target="_blank">sutemos.net</a></p> Tags: <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/batti" title="batti" rel="tag">batti</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/download" title="download" rel="tag">download</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/pop" title="Pop" rel="tag">Pop</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/progressive" title="progressive" rel="tag">progressive</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/rock" title="Rock" rel="tag">Rock</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/sebastian-borg" title="Sebastian Borg" rel="tag">Sebastian Borg</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/stockfinster" title="Stockfinster" rel="tag">Stockfinster</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/sutemos" title="Sutemos" rel="tag">Sutemos</a><br /> <h4>Related posts</h4> <ul class="st-related-posts"> <li><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/pop/498-va-sweets-for-the-wild-3-another-record" title="V.A. &#8211;           <itunes:keywords>batti,download,Pop,progressive,Rock,Sebastian Borg,Stockfinster,Sutemos<itunes:keywords/>
          <itunes:subtitle>Epic Electronic Prog Pop | The Lithuanian Netlabel Sutemos is nothing new to you most likely. We have been covering their outcome ever since. Stockfinster, all the same, is a name commonly known to fans of free music.<itunes:subtitle/>
          <itunes:summary>(http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/stockfinster_dead_line-250x250.jpg)Epic Electronic Prog Pop | The Lithuanian Netlabel Sutemos is nothing new to you most likely. We have been covering their outcome ever (http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/ambient/1036-various-intelligent-toys-5-sutemos-netlabel) since (http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/idm/1486-ijo-selektida-sutemos). Stockfinster, all the same, is a name commonly known to fans of free music. After the debut "All Becomes Music" was released in 2005, it took four years to complete "Dead Line", the novel full-lenght of album of Stockfinster. A long time waiting, but worth the years without a doubt. Stockfinster - "Push Push" (MP3) (http://www.archive.org/download//Stockfinster.-DeadLinesutemos025/01_Push_Push.mp3) Stockfinster - "Knuckle" (MP3) (http://www.archive.org/download//Stockfinster.-DeadLinesutemos025/05_Knuckle.mp3) Stockfinster- "Gold Canyon" (MP3) (http://www.archive.org/download//Stockfinster.-DeadLinesutemos025/06_Gold_Canyon.mp3) Stockfinster- "Mitglieder" (MP3) (http://www.archive.org/download//Stockfinster.-DeadLinesutemos025/07_Mitglieder.mp3) Stockfinster (German for "pitch black") is the one man band of MalmÃ¶-based Sebastian Borg. In the liner notes to "Dead Line", Borg (who commonly appears as "batti") excuses himself for being unproductive and slow. However, for a 76 minutes opus magnus, perfectly arranged and composed like this, many musicians need a whole lifetime for. If any. The music of Stockfinster is a mixture of Postrock and progressive Pop, essentially enhanced by many electronic elements. There is an element of nostalgia to Borg's music that stems from his melancholic melodies and the late 90's breakbeat patterns. Several time I had to think of early Lamb or other forward-thinking "Trip Hop" acts. From the world of Netaudio, Orange Crush (http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/hiphop/1164-orange-crush-autumn-reflections-archaic-horizon), Endless (http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/electronica-indietronic/111-endlos-kein-grund-zufrieden-zu-sein-live-ep-1bit-wonder) or Nic Bommaritio (http://www.12rec.net/Release_Nic-Bommarito_Harp-Fragments_058.htm) might suit for comparison. Albeit not actually at the edge of contemporary music, Stockfinster has something more valuable to offer: timelessness. Strong, atmospheric melodies, impellent beats, and a supreme production. Should be OK for the next four years, no? MP3 Pop Music Download Download: "Dead Line" (http://www.archive.org/download/Stockfinster.-DeadLinesutemos025/Sutemos025.zip) (ZIP-Archive) Artist-Website: stockfinster.nu (http://www.stockfinster.nu/) Release: Stockfinster - "Dead Line" (http://www.sutemos.net/en/release;gid,27) Netlabel: sutemos.net (http://www.sutemos.net/)<itunes:summary/>

          <content:encoded><p><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/cover_600_ebc004_front.jpg"><img class="alignleft size-medium wp-image-1632" title="cover_600_ebc004_front" src="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/cover_600_ebc004_front-250x250.jpg" alt="" width="250" height="250" /></a><strong>Glitchy Chipfunk Hipedihop Music</strong> | OK, let's get down once again with the Error Broadcast Crew. Open the windows of your hipster car and let the sounds cover the streets with a heavy dose of subbass, quirky and glitchy bleeps and funk. Meister Pixelord knows how to build some wonky beats and bass. His debut brings you some chipmusic-inspired hip hop instrumentals Mario would loved to stumble upon while jumping his way through the next level.</p> <p><!--mp3links--><br /> <a href="http://error-broadcast.com/releases/ebc004/ebc004_pixelord_01_cartoon_friend.mp3">Pixelord - "Cartoon Friend" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://error-broadcast.com/releases/ebc004/ebc004_pixelord_02_quartz_boy.mp3">Pixelord - "Quartz Boy" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://error-broadcast.com/releases/ebc004/ebc004_pixelord_03_cybernator.mp3">Pixelord - "Cybernator" (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://error-broadcast.com/releases/ebc004/ebc004_pixelord_04_boss_worm.mp3">Pixelord - "Bosworm" (MP3)</a><br /> <!--mp3linksend--></p> <p><span id="more-1631"></span></p> <p><!--adsense--></p> <p>The Pixelord is Moscow-based musician Alexey Devyanin. To some he is known as Gultskra Artikler. Under this moniker he produced some freaky experimental music. Now, he tickles the knobs of his synthesizers and mixer to squeeze out some extraordinary and truly funky hip hop I've never listen to before in that kind of combination.</p> <p>"Lucid Freaks pt. 1" is a perfect cocktail of chip music funk flickering over solid beats, staggering like a drunken monk.           <content:encoded><p><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/cover_henrik_jose_little_things.jpg"><img src="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/cover_henrik_jose_little_things-250x250.jpg" alt="" class="alignleft size-medium wp-image-1628" title="cover_henrik_jose_little_things" width="250" height="250" /></a><strong>Spherical Pop</strong> | Last year one musician appeared on the chart lists of a lot of netaudio musiclovers: Henrik JosÃ© from MalmÃ¶, Sweden. We loved his pop anthem "Possibilities" so much, we had to include it on our <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/free-compilation/1619-music-from-all-around-the-world">free music compilation "Music From All Around The World"</a>. And just some seconds later, he releases a new wonderful small album on Swedens brightest netlabel: 23 Seconds. <em>Hurray!</em></p> <p><!--mp3links--><br /> <a href="http://www.23seconds.org/01%20-%20Rich%20And%20Timeless.mp3">Rich And Timeless (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.23seconds.org/02%20-%20Pinpointing%20The%20Problem.mp3">Pinpointing The Problem (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.23seconds.org/03%20-%20The%20Little%20Things.mp3">The Little Things (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.23seconds.org/04%20-%20Magnet%20In%20My%20Mouth.mp3">Magnet In My Mouth (MP3)</a><br /> <a href="http://www.23seconds.org/05%20-%20We%20Own%20This%20Thing.mp3">We Own This Thing (MP3)</a><br /> <!--mp3linksend--></p> <p><span id="more-1629"></span></p> <p><!--adsense--></p> <p>Henrik JosÃ© is also known for his moniker Bliss. And we music geeks know: Henrik JosÃ© is no stranger to the world of free music. But while he explored IDM and Electronica under the cover of Bliss, he opens up under his real name. And during this process everything seems to fall into place.</p> <p>All the wonderful melodies he composed already years ago now meet the world of pop. If you listen closely to his five songs you also discover the tricks and twists in his games with beats. Here's someone who grew up, but who doesn't neglets his past. Here's someone who won't forget his love for Electronica and IDM. The only thing that changed, is that everything in the name of pop got a little bit more forward. Instead of shreddering beats up, we listen to the true voice, a voice that wants to tell us some stories.</p> <p>This is pure electrifying electronic pop without citation of the 80ies. No, it's pop plus electronic music on an individual level. Welcome to the melancholic and melodic soundscapes of Henrik JosÃ©.</p> <h2>MP3 Pop Music Download</h2> <p><strong>Download:</strong> <a href="http://www.23seconds.org/%5Bsec.041%5DHenrik%20Jose%20-%20The%20Little%20Things%20EP.zip">Henrik JosÃ© - "The Little Things EP" (ZIP-Archive)</a><br /> <strong>Artist-Website:</strong> <a href="http://www.henrikjose.com/">www.henrikjose.com</a><br /> <strong>Release:</strong> <a href="http://www.23seconds.org/041.htm">Henrik JosÃ© - "The Little Things EP"</a><br /> <strong>Netlabel:</strong> <a href="http://www.23seconds.org/">23 Seconds Netlabel</a></p> <p>Free, MP3, Music, Download, Netlabel,</p> Tags: <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/23-seconds" title="23 Seconds" rel="tag">23 Seconds</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/bliss" title="Bliss" rel="tag">Bliss</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/electronica" title="electronica" rel="tag">electronica</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/henrik-jose" title="henrik jose" rel="tag">henrik jose</a>, <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/tag/pop" title="Pop" rel="tag">Pop</a><br /> <h4>Related posts</h4> <ul class="st-related-posts"> <li><a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/electronica-indietronic/1064-xydzo-puls" title="XYDZO &#8211;           <description><p>Our Phlow Compilation "Music From All Around The World" is prove, that you find wonderful creative commons pop music. It's prove that free has nothing to do with low quality or geeky dark ambient. On top of all "Music From All Around The World" shows that the worldwide creative commons music scene offers more and more compatible music be played out loud on the radio. We at Phlow believe that 2010 creative commons music will please more and more music lovers who love songs, vocals and pop in general. <a href="http://phlow-magazine.com/mp3-music-download/free-compilation/1619-music-from-all-around-the-world">Download our free pop music compilation!</a></p><description/>
          <content:encoded><p><img src="http://phlow-magazine.com/wp-content/uploads/cover_music_from_all_around_the_world.jpg" alt="Cover Artwork by Jeannette Corneille" width="580" height="580" /><strong>Pop Music Compilation</strong> | Our Phlow Compilation "Music From All Around The World" is prove, that you find wonderful creative commons pop music. It's prove that free has nothing to do with low quality or geeky dark ambient. On top of all <strong>"Music From All Around The World" shows that the worldwide creative commons music scene offers more and more compatible music be played out loud on the radio.</strong> We at Phlow believe that 2010 creative commons music will please more and more music lovers who love songs, vocals and pop in general.</strong><span id="more-1619"></span></p> <p>With average music listeners in mind, who don't get lost with excitement in dusty box at their record dealer of choice we crafted this compilation. We made our girlfriend listen to the music, asked her for advice and offer you now a true pop music compilation for people who enjoy some happy melodies.</p> <p>Smile with us listening to melancholic songs from The Black Atlantic or Jsvenes y Sexys from South America. Please push your chair aside and dance to some disco music from Comfort Fit and Opolopo and clap your hands with that four to the floor beat. Laugh about the mad rhymes by Tracky Birthday and get mad with Professor Kliq. Get down with some some downtempo hip hop from fLako and B-Ju and rise your hands again into the air with Henrik Jose.</p> <h2>Playlist ofÂ  "Music From All Around The World"</h2> <ol> <li><a href="http://mp3.phlow.de/compilation/music_from_all_around_the_world/01._music_from_all_around_the_world_-_soto_-_orange.mp3"><strong>Soto -
